- to provide technical support and advice to users;

- to perform quality control for the production maintenance and the enhancement of the application systems of C&ED;
- Meeting / working at remote locations, such as other C&ED offices and land boundary control points, is required;
- The candidate is required to provide service outside office hours, e.g. 7 x 24 on-call production support;
- The candidate may require to work at C&ED remote offices scattered over the territory such as control points for support;
- Integrity record check for the candidate is required and the candidate shall be requested to sign a consent during the recruitment interview.
